function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.431!');
}

	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_8();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'c5e2fbbd42d4e745f4ee44f7105db6091726f7c0') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'c5e2fbbd42d4e745f4ee44f7105db6091726f7c0') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '40578c35b31f840da228c22904da6bc086e73cab') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'c5e2fbbd42d4e745f4ee44f7105db6091726f7c0') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/config_values.txt');
	writefile_9();
	if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') != '62af348d22ce9a2b6a2ba293fa7bfd9493bb27cd') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/config_values.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/config_values.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== '62af348d22ce9a2b6a2ba293fa7bfd9493bb27cd') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'b2037dce784ccd0d8c8850981307e49b1c40cff7') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/config_values.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/config_values.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/config_values.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/config_values.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_9();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== '62af348d22ce9a2b6a2ba293fa7bfd9493bb27cd') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_11();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != 'c5de6ea5e35fa407409afad8757a3d6ed4b8736a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'c5de6ea5e35fa407409afad8757a3d6ed4b8736a') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '674a75456c56deef5199a20670a210a31ea74173') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'c5de6ea5e35fa407409afad8757a3d6ed4b8736a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

// Files different: plugins/publicPages/800_login_ldap/manifest.xml

		if (@sha1_file('plugins/raPages/102_change_email/OIDplusPageRaChangeEMail.class.php') !== 'aa900a941ca4031bcf30e77944561fc675daf51a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/raPages/102_change_email/OIDplusPageRaChangeEMail.class.php');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 432\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 432') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
